      </div> 
      <p><b>Pornography laws by region</b> vary throughout the world. The production and distribution of <a href="/wiki/Pornographic_film" title="Pornographic film">pornographic films</a> are both activities that are lawful in many, but by no means all, countries so long as the <a href="/wiki/Pornography" title="Pornography">pornography</a> features performers aged <a href="/wiki/Age_of_majority" title="Age of majority">above a certain age</a>, usually eighteen years. Further restrictions are often placed on such material. </p>
      <p>This page excludes <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography" title="Child pornography">child pornography</a>, which in most cases is treated as a separate kind of pornography. </p>

            Article 263. (Illegal dissemination of pornographic materials or items)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;">
             Illegal manufacture, sale as well as, dissemination of pornographic materials or items, as well as, printed publications, films and videos, images or other pornographic objects, and advertising, is punished with a fine in the amount of 200 to 400 minimal salaries, or with arrest for the term of up to 2 months, or with imprisonment for the term of up to 2 years

         <td><a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Blocked </td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 381. (Lewd and lascivious conduct )
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;">
             A defendant shall be guilty of the offence of lewd and lascivious conduct, if the defendant:
            <br> (b) Sells, manufactures, issues, distributes, displays or otherwise deals in obscene material. 
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 476. (Computer pornography )
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;">
             A defendant shall be guilty of the offence of computer pornography, if the defendant:
            <br> (a) Publishes and distributes an obscene photograph or picture on the computer or over the internet; or
            <br> (b) Is an internet service provider, who knowingly acts as a host for pornographic material or acts as a channel for the image to be transmitted to an individual user. 
           </div>
          </div> </td> 
         <td><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> </td>

            Article 292. (Sale etc. of obscene articles)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Whoever sells, lets to hire, distributes, publicly exhibits or in any manner puts into circulation, or for purposes of sale, hire distribution, public exhibition or circulation makes, produces or has in his possession any obscene article shall be guilty of an offence and shall be punished with a fine of not less than $500 and not more than $5,000 and imprisonment which may extend to 2 years; and in the case of a second or subsequent conviction, a fine of not less than $1,000 and not more than $30,000 and imprisonment which may extend to 5 years. </li>
            </ol>

         <td><a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a></td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Blocked</td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 313. (Obscene or Indecent Publications)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>A person who publicly distributes, displays or traffics in writings, images, posters, films, possession, objects or other communications that are obscene or grossly indecent, is guilty of obscenity, a Class 1 petty offence, punishable with a definite term of imprisonment of not less than 6 months and not more than 12 months, or a fine of 20,001 – 50,000 <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_nakfa" title="Eritrean nakfa">Nakfas</a>, to be set in intervals of 2,500 Nakfas.</li> 
             <li>It is not an offence under sub-Article (1) where the conduct takes place in private, or where the material is artistic, literary or scientific in character. </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
          </div> </td> 
         <td> </td>

        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a></td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal, but manufacturing and distribution illegal.</td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Most porn sites are banned</td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Indian Penal Code-1860 Section 292, 293 and IT Act-67B. (Illegal dissemination of pornographic materials) &amp; (Illegal Child Pornography)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Anyone who sells, let's to hire, distributes, exhibits or circulates to any person under the age of 20 years any such obscene object a Illegal manufacture, sale as well as, dissemination of pornographic materials or items, as well as, printed publications will severely punished with a fine in the amount of 2000 <a href="/wiki/Indian_rupee" title="Indian rupee">rupees</a> fine for monthly term, or with imprisonment for the term of up to 7 years.</li> 
             <li>Whoever browses, publishes, creates, downloads obscene content of child pornography which are strictly prohibited will be punished with imprisonment of 5 years and 10 lakh <a href="/wiki/Indian_rupee" title="Indian rupee">rupees</a> fine. </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
          </div> </td> 
         <td><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a></td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Blocked</td> 
         <td> 
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            <i>Undang-Undang Republik Indonesia No. 44 Tahun 2008 tentang Pornografi, Pasal 29 dan 32</i> (Republic of Indonesia Law No. 44 Year 2008 on Pornography, Article 29 and 32)<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup>
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <p><b><i>Pasal 29</i> (Article 29)</b> </p>
            <p><i>Setiap orang yang memproduksi, membuat, memperbanyak, menggandakan, menyebarluaskan, menyiarkan, mengimpor, mengekspor, menawarkan, memperjualbelikan, menyewakan, atau menyediakan pornografi sebagaimana dimaksud dalam Pasal 4 ayat (1) dipidana dengan pidana penjara paling singkat 6 (enam) bulan dan paling lama 12 (dua belas) tahun dan/atau pidana denda paling sedikit Rp250.000.000,00 (dua ratus lima puluh juta rupiah) dan paling banyak Rp6.000.000.000,00 (enam miliar rupiah).</i> (Every person who produces, makes, reproduces, duplicates, spreads, airs, imports, exports, offers, trades, rents, or provides pornography as meant in Article 4 paragraph (1) shall be punished with imprisonment of at least 6 (six) months and at most 12 (twelve) years and/or a fine of at least Rp250.000.000,00 (two hundred fifty million rupiah) and at most Rp6.000.000.000,00 (six billion rupiah).) </p>
            <p><b><i>Pasal 32</i> (Article 32)</b> </p> <i>Setiap orang yang memperdengarkan, mempertontonkan, memanfaatkan, memiliki, atau menyimpan produk pornografi sebagaimana dimaksud dalam Pasal 6 dipidana dengan pidana penjara paling lama 4 (empat) tahun dan/atau pidana denda paling banyak Rp2.000.000.000,00 (dua miliar rupiah).</i> (Every person who plays, displays, utilizes, possesses, or stores pornographic products as meant in Article 6 shall be punished with imprisonment of up to 4 (four) years and/or a fine of at least Rp250.000.000,00 (two hundred fifty million rupiah) and at most Rp6.000.000.000,00 (6 billion rupiah).) 
           </div>
          </div> </td> 
         <td>,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> and see: <a href="/wiki/Bill_against_Pornography_and_Pornoaction" title="Bill against Pornography and Pornoaction">Bill against Pornography and Pornoaction</a> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal </td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 166. (Traffic in obscene publication)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Any person who: <br> (a) for the purpose of or by way of trade or for the purpose of distribution or public exhibition, makes, produces or has in his possession any one or more obscene writings, drawings, prints, paintings, printed matter, pictures, posters, emblems, photographs, cinematograph -films or any other objects or any other object tending to corrupt morals [...]<br>&nbsp;: is guilty of a misdemeanour, and is liable, to imprisonment for two years or to a fine of seven thousand <a href="/wiki/Kenyan_shilling" title="Kenyan shilling">shillings</a>.</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> </td>

           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>A person commits an offense if, with knowledge of its obscene nature or content, he:</li>
            </ol>

            <hr> (6) Creates, buys, procures, or possesses obscene matter or material with the purpose of distributing it in violation of this Section. [...] The offenses in Subsections (a)(1) through (a)(6) are Class 1 misdemeanors. 
           </div>

           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Any person who: <br> (a) for the purpose of or by way of trade or for the purpose of distribution or public exhibition, makes, produces or has in his possession any one or more obscene writings, drawings, prints, paintings, printed matter, pictures, posters, emblems, photographs, cinematograph -films or any other objects or any other object tending to corrupt morals [...]<br>&nbsp;: is guilty of a misdemeanour, and is liable, to imprisonment for two years or to a fine of two hundred dollars.</li>

         <td><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal </td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Limitedly legal </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Blocked </td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 243 (Distribution, etc. of Obscene Pictures)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Any person who distributes, sells, lends, openly displays or shows any obscene documents, drawing, pictures, films or other things, shall be punished by imprisonment for not more than one year or by a fine not exceeding five million won.</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 244 (Manufacture, etc. of Obscene Pictures)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>A person who, for the purpose of accomplishing the acts as prescribed in Article 243, manufactures, possesses, imports or exports obscene goods, shall be punished by imprisonment for not more than one year or by a fine not exceeding five million won.</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 44-7 (Prohibition on Circulation of Unlawful Information)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>No one may circulate any of the following information through an information and communications network: 1. Information with obscene content distributed, sold, rented, or displayed openly in the form of code, words, sound, images, or motion picture;</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> </td> 
         <td><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Blocked </td> 
         <td>
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 285. (Sale, &amp;c. of obscene books .&amp;c.)
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Whoever sells or distributes, imports, or prints for sale or hire, or wilfully exhibits to public view, any obscene book, pamphlet, paper, drawing, painting, photograph, representation, or figure, or attempts or offers so to do, shall be punished with imprisonment of either description for a term which may extend to three months, or with fine, or with both.</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;text-align:center;">
           <div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:center;;background:#ccccff">
            Article 286. (Having in possession obscene books, &amp;c for sale or public exhibition. )
           </div>
           <div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;"> 
            <ol>
             <li>Whoever has in his possession any such obscene book or other thing as is mentioned in the last preceding section for the purpose of sale, distribution, or public exhibition, shall be punished with imprisonment of either description for a term which may extend to three months. Or with fine, or with both.</li>
            </ol> 
           </div>
          </div> </td>
