      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Africa">Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Botswana">Botswana</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Botswana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The possession of "Indecent and obscene material such as pornographic books, magazines, films, videos, DVDs and software" is prohibited in <a href="/wiki/Botswana" title="Botswana">Botswana</a>. Possession or import of such material is illegal and punishable by a fine or up to 4 years' imprisonment.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Egypt">Egypt</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Egypt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>, it is illegal to distribute pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> The possession and import of pornography are offences.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> Unlike numerous African nations which have no laws against child pornography, <a href="/wiki/Internet_in_Egypt" title="Internet in Egypt">Egypt blocks child pornography websites</a> and dealing in child pornography carries a minimum sentence of five years and fines of US$29,000.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> In 2009 Egypt's Administrative Court ruled that internet pornography should be banned, describing it as "venomous and vile". In 2012 the country's Prosecutor General ordered government ministries to block the websites.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> However, the cost of blocking large numbers of pornographic websites has prevented the full implementation of the court's ruling.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Ethiopia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Distributing or selling pornographic materials is illegal in Ethiopia, and their production in the country is rare. There are no official laws regarding Internet pornography in Ethiopia making the Internet the only available source of pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Morocco">Morocco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Morocco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In 2004, Morocco introduced severe punishment for promoting pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> Producing pornography of any kind is illegal in Morocco. However, pornographic websites are widely accessible in Morocco.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nigeria">Nigeria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Nigeria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Nigeria has no national laws prohibiting pornography, although the public display of graphic sexual material is illegal in Lagos. The country has a small indigenous pornography industry which produces exclusively heterosexual pornography as <a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_in_Nigeria" title="LGBT rights in Nigeria">homosexual activity in Nigeria is illegal</a>. Some Muslim politicians in the national government have proposed a nationwide block on pornographic websites.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> There is significant piracy of pornography in Nigeria, with pirated pornographic DVDs being sold from roadside stalls in <a href="/wiki/Lagos" title="Lagos">Lagos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> Pornography is also sold in Nigerian <a href="/wiki/Sex_shop" title="Sex shop">sex shops</a> and some <a href="/wiki/Pornographic_magazine" title="Pornographic magazine">pornographic magazines</a> are produced in the country, often reproducing pictures from foreign magazines. The first officially acknowledged <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_pornography" title="Hardcore pornography">hardcore pornographic</a> film produced in Nigeria was <i>Better Lover Valentine Sex Party</i>. It was not submitted to the National Film and Video Censors Board for classification and it was immediately banned on the grounds of obscenity and immorality.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> Internet pornography is widely viewed in Nigeria. In 2015 the monthly average for the number of searches for pornography was 135,000, and in December 2014 and 2015 the proportion of searches for pornography (relative to other searches) was higher in Nigeria than in the United States. In 2013 Nigeria ranked second globally for Internet searches for <a href="/wiki/Gay_pornography" title="Gay pornography">gay pornography</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Somalia">Somalia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Somalia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>There are no laws regarding pornography in Somalia, although displaying it in public is considered a crime. There are no adult stores. However all pornographic websites are freely available.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Africa">South Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: South Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography rated X18 is permitted by the law only if sold to persons over the age of 18 in registered stores. It is an offense to host a pornographic web site in South Africa because of the difficulty of age-verification and the requirement that pornography only be distributed from designated, licensed physical premises. It is also unlawful to visually represent bestiality (also rated XX), but not in text descriptions. Supplying violent pornography is an offence in any form, but the law allows the production of pornography that is not prohibited. </p>
      <p>Distribution of pornography is regulated by the Films and Publications Act of 1996,<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> which is enforced by the Films and Publications Board.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sudan">Sudan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Sudan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography is prohibited in Sudan and the laws are strict. Pornographic websites are blocked by the government, pornography is largely inaccessible, and porn possession, production, distribution and sale can lead to fines, prison or <a href="/wiki/Corporal_punishment" title="Corporal punishment">corporal punishment</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Uganda">Uganda</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Uganda">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornographic DVDs have in the past been sold on the streets in <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Fallon_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fallon-46">[46]</a></sup> However, an Anti-Pornography Act (popularly known as the "Anti-Miniskirt Law") was signed into law in 2014 with the stated objectives of defining what constitutes the offence of pornography and establishing a Pornography Control Committee.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup> The committee is responsible for the implementation of the law and for taking measures to detect, prohibit, collect and destroy pornographic materials.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup> The law broadly defines pornography as "any representation of the sexual parts of a person for primarily sexual excitement".<sup id="cite_ref-Fallon_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fallon-46">[46]</a></sup> The law says that "a person shall not produce, traffic in, publish, broadcast, procure, import, export, sell or abet any form of pornography". Breaches of the law are punishable with up to ten years in jail.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup> Prior to the passing of the act there were a number of laws concerning aspects of pornography in Uganda, but this was the first law to create a specific offence of pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> The law repeals and replaces Section 166 of the Penal Code Act, widening the legal interpretation of pornography and prohibiting it comprehensively.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> The law has been subject to challenge in the Constitutional Court on the basis of its vague wording and the broad powers of the committee.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In July 2018, the Ugandan government directed the country's ISPs to block 27 pornographic websites.<sup id="cite_ref-uganda_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uganda-30">[30]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Americas">Americas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Americas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_the_Americas" title="Pornography in the Americas">Pornography in the Americas</a>
      </div> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bahamas">Bahamas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Bahamas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The Bahamian penal code prohibits the production and distribution of obscene publications.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> Many types of pornography are prohibited in the Bahamas; however, law enforcement is relaxed and does not usually enforce the prohibition.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Self-published_sources" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on a self-published source. (February 2020)">self-published source?</span></a></i>]</sup> Pornography is available on Bahamian cable television<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> and in 2014 <a href="/wiki/ZNS-TV" title="ZNS-TV">ZNS-TV</a> broadcast a report on the establishment of a local pornography industry in the Bahamas.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil">Brazil</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Brazil">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In Brazil, <a href="/wiki/Pornographic_film_actor" title="Pornographic film actor">pornographic film actors</a> must be 18 or older. Pornography which does not involve bestiality is legal when sold in public places. Depiction of sex with animals is illegal. And DVD covers that depict genitalia must not be visible to public view, and pornography can only be sold to people 18 or older. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Canada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Canada" title="Pornography in Canada">Pornography in Canada</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The laws of Canada permit the sale of <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_pornography" title="Hardcore pornography">hardcore pornography</a> to anyone over the age of eighteen. While persons below that age may have pornography in their possession, its sale to them is prohibited. </p>
      <p>Most hardcore pornography is sold in <a href="/wiki/Sex_shop" title="Sex shop">adult stores</a> or on <a href="/wiki/Internet_pornography" title="Internet pornography">adult websites</a>. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">Cuba</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Cuba">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography was illegal in Cuba during <a href="/wiki/Fidel_Castro" title="Fidel Castro">Fidel Castro</a>'s leadership of the country, but the laws were relaxed in the 2010s.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> However, many pornographic websites are still blocked in Cuba.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Guyana">Guyana</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Guyana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a>, it is illegal to sell or possess pornography. Distribution, possession, sale, and importation of pornographic magazines, DVDs, books, photographs, etc. or simply browsing for pornographic websites on the Internet can lead to a variety of punishments ranging from community service, a fine of up to 45,000 Guyana dollars, up to 2 years in prison, or <a href="/wiki/Corporal_punishment" title="Corporal punishment">corporal punishment</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jamaica">Jamaica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Jamaica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography is legal in Jamaica for adults over 18, but age verifications for buying porn or any sex-related products are relatively lax. The Jamaican government is planning to block Internet child pornography.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">Mexico</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Mexico">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>From early on in the 20th century <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> was known for producing a lot of films with full female nudity and softcore pornographic scenes.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">United States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: United States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_the_United_States" title="Pornography in the United States">Pornography in the United States</a>
      </div> 
      <p>In the United States, pornography is not unlawful at the federal level, but is subject to the <a href="/wiki/Miller_test" title="Miller test"><i>Miller</i> test</a>, which was developed in the 1973 case <i><a href="/wiki/Miller_v._California" title="Miller v. California">Miller v. California</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> The Miller test was an effort to differentiate between pornography and 'obscenity.' It has three parts: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>Whether "the average person, applying contemporary <a href="/wiki/Community_standards" title="Community standards">community standards</a>", would find that the <a href="/wiki/Work_of_art" title="Work of art">work</a>, taken as a whole, appeals to the <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prurient" class="extiw" title="wikt:prurient">prurient</a> interest,</li> 
       <li>Whether the work depicts or describes, in a <a href="/wiki/Patently_offensive" title="Patently offensive">patently offensive</a> way, sexual conduct specifically defined by applicable state law,</li> 
       <li>Whether the work, taken as a whole, lacks serious <a href="/wiki/Literature" title="Literature">literary</a>, <a href="/wiki/Art" title="Art">artistic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Politics" title="Politics">political</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Science" title="Science">scientific</a> value.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>The work is considered obscene only if <i>all three</i> conditions are satisfied. Local areas are permitted to develop their own laws on the issue, as long as they do not conflict with federal law. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Asia">Asia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Asia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Asia" title="Pornography in Asia">Pornography in Asia</a>
      </div> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Bangladesh">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Bangladesh" title="Pornography in Bangladesh">Pornography in Bangladesh</a>
      </div> 
      <p>By passing the "Pornography Control Act, 2012", the government of Bangladesh prohibited the carrying, exchanging, using, selling, marketing, distributing, preserving, filming etc. of pornography (sexually explicit materials, unless it has artistic and/or educational value). Penalties include a maximum of 10 years in prison and fines up to Tk.500,000/(US$6,410) </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_China" title="Pornography in China">Pornography in China</a>
      </div> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mainland">Mainland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Mainland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4> 
      <p>It is illegal to sell or distribute pornography in mainland China, but it is not illegal to own or to watch it. Google, Yahoo, YouTube and other websites do not allow users in China to perform searches related to sex.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> Pornographic material in mainland China comes from Hong Kong, Macau, Taiwan, or Japan.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Hong Kong">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4> 
      <p>Pornographic films in Hong Kong are referred to as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Hong_Kong_Category_III_films" title="List of Hong Kong Category III films">Category III films</a>, after the territory's motion picture rating system. Category III films would generally be considered softcore by American and Japanese standards, often featuring more elaborate and comical plots than foreign equivalents. In the early 21st century many of the roles involving sex scenes are actually performed by Japanese actresses, with any dialogue dubbed into Cantonese, rather than by local actresses. </p>
      <p>Hardcore pornographic videos and films, in both physical and digital forms, can be legally sold in the territory. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: India">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_India" title="Pornography in India">Pornography in India</a>
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>The selling and distribution of <a href="/wiki/Pornography" title="Pornography">pornographic material</a> is illegal in India under section 292<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>The distribution, sale, or circulation of obscene materials and the selling of pornographic content to any person under age 20 years are illegal under section 293 and IT Act-67B.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>Child pornography is illegal and strictly prohibited across the country under section 67B of the <a href="/wiki/Information_Technology_Act,_2000" title="Information Technology Act, 2000">Information Technology Act, 2000</a><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>The manufacturing, publishing and distribution of pornography is illegal in India under section 292, 293.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>In July 2015 the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_India" title="Supreme Court of India">Supreme Court of India</a> refused to allow the blocking of pornographic websites and said that watching pornography indoors in the privacy of one's own home was not a crime.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> In August 2015 the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_India" title="Government of India">Government of India</a> issued an order to Indian ISPs to block at least 857 websites that it considered to be pornographic.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> In 2015 the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Telecommunications" title="Department of Telecommunications">Department of Telecommunications</a> (DoT) had asked internet service providers to take down 857 websites in a bid to control cyber crime, but after receiving criticism from the authorities it partially rescinded the ban. The ban from the government came after a lawyer filed a petition in the Supreme Court arguing that online pornography encourages sex crimes and rapes.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In February 2016 the Supreme Court asked the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Government" class="mw-redirect" title="Indian Government">Indian Government</a> to suggest ways of banning all forms of child pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In October 2018 the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_India" title="Government of India">government</a> directed Internet service providers to block 827 websites that host pornographic content following an order by the <a href="/wiki/Uttarakhand_High_Court" title="Uttarakhand High Court">Uttarakhand High Court</a>. The court cited the rape of a 10th standard girl from <a href="/wiki/Dehradun" title="Dehradun">Dehradun</a> by four of her seniors. The four accused told police that they raped the girl after watching pornography on the Internet.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Japan">Japan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Japan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Japan" title="Pornography in Japan">Pornography in Japan</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Pornography is legal in Japan; however, there are restrictions. <a href="/wiki/Sex_organ" title="Sex organ">Genitalia</a> must be pixelated or censored and all participants must be 18 years of age or older. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lebanon">Lebanon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Lebanon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography in Lebanon is illegal and is subject to several legal provisions, but it's considered legal to access pornographic websites for personal use only.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nepal">Nepal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Nepal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Nepali law identifies pornography as illegal. The sharing, distribution and broadcasting of pornographic content through any medium is prohibited.<sup id="cite_ref-Samiti_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Samiti-17">[17]</a></sup> In 2010 it was reported that the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Home_Affairs_(Nepal)" title="Ministry of Home Affairs (Nepal)">Home Ministry</a> had banned access to a list of websites including explicitly adult websites.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup> In September 2018, concerns about <a href="/wiki/Violence_against_women" title="Violence against women">violence against women</a> led the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Nepal" title="Government of Nepal">Government of Nepal</a> to announce its intention to ban online pornography.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> From 24 September, the <a href="/wiki/Nepal_Telecommunications_Authority" title="Nepal Telecommunications Authority">Nepal Telecommunications Authority</a> (NTA) began to put a block on all websites providing pornographic content on the orders of the Nepal Government <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Information_and_Communications_(Nepal)" title="Ministry of Information and Communications (Nepal)">Ministry of Communication and Information Technology</a> (MOCIT). By 12 October more than 21,000 pornographic websites had been blocked.<sup id="cite_ref-Samiti_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Samiti-17">[17]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Korea">North Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: North Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_North_Korea" title="Pornography in North Korea">Pornography in North Korea</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Both domestic and imported works of <a href="/wiki/Pornography" title="Pornography">pornography</a> have been available in <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> since recent decades.<sup id="cite_ref-Shin2015_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shin2015-71">[71]</a></sup> Producing, distributing, importing and watching pornography is prohibited.<sup id="cite_ref-HassigOh2015_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HassigOh2015-72">[72]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Possession of pornography became widespread among elites during the late 1990s. Political and army elites are the most active consumers of pornography. Locally produced pornography initially appeared during the reign of <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a>. A typical North Korean-made <a href="/wiki/Pornographic_film" title="Pornographic film">pornographic film</a> involves nude or scantily clad women dancing with music.<sup id="cite_ref-Moon2007_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moon2007-73">[73]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Importing pornography to North Korea is harshly punished. Pornography is sold openly on the <a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93North_Korea_border" title="China–North Korea border">China–North Korea border</a> regardless of regulations.<sup id="cite_ref-Schwartzman2009_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Schwartzman2009-74">[74]</a></sup> Despite attempts to curtail circulation of imported pornography, most of the pornography watched in North Korea is currently made abroad.<sup id="cite_ref-Moon2007_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moon2007-73">[73]</a></sup> A significant part of pornographic media in circulation consists of Chinese <a href="/wiki/Bootleg_recording" title="Bootleg recording">bootleg recordings</a> of poor quality.<sup id="cite_ref-Shin2015_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shin2015-71">[71]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>There is <a href="/wiki/Censorship_in_North_Korea" title="Censorship in North Korea">no access</a> to foreign pornographic websites from within North Korea.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>North Korea has ratified the <a href="/wiki/Optional_Protocol_on_the_Sale_of_Children,_Child_Prostitution_and_Child_Pornography" title="Optional Protocol on the Sale of Children, Child Prostitution and Child Pornography">Optional Protocol on the Sale of Children, Child Prostitution and Child Pornography</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Convention_on_the_Rights_of_the_Child" title="Convention on the Rights of the Child">Convention on the Rights of the Child</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> However, there are currently no specific laws to combat <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography" title="Child pornography">child pornography</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Korea">South Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: South Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Further information: <a href="/wiki/Internet_censorship_in_South_Korea" title="Internet censorship in South Korea">Internet censorship in South Korea</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Pornography is banned by the government in South Korea, with laws strictly enforced. The distribution, sale or display of obscene materials via the Internet can be punished with up to two years' imprisonment, although there is no penalty for watching or possessing Internet pornography, <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">except in some counties of provinces and cities near North Korea where neither possession nor distribution is allowed.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The exception is child pornography, the possession of which carries a maximum one-year prison sentence, and the maximum sentence for distributing, selling or displaying it for commercial purposes is ten years. Many foreign pornographic websites are blocked, and those found to be operating from within the country are shut down.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> The Korea Internet Safety Commission is responsible for instructing <a href="/wiki/Internet_service_provider" title="Internet service provider">Internet service providers</a> to block access to "pornography and nudity".<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Google_Search" title="Google Search">Google Search</a> in South Korea filters search results for around 700 terms considered by the government to be adult in nature unless the user demonstrates that they are aged over 19.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan">Pakistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Pakistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Pakistan" title="Pornography in Pakistan">Pornography in Pakistan</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Pornography in Pakistan is illegal and is subject to several legal provisions. Since November 2011 the Government has placed a complete ban on Internet websites containing pornographic material. The list of banned websites is updated on an ongoing basis. In 2019 Pakistan's Human Rights Minister, <a href="/wiki/Shireen_Mazari" title="Shireen Mazari">Shireen Mazari</a>, said that Pakistan was ranked as the country with the largest numbers of <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography" title="Child pornography">child pornography</a> viewers, although this has yet to be verified.<sup id="cite_ref-HRM_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HRM-81">[81]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIA_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIA-82">[82]</a></sup> Despite this, child pornography is illegal and strictly forbidden in Pakistan and there are severe punishments for possessing or viewing child pornography which include a minimum of 14 years to 20 years in prison and a fine of 1 million <a href="/wiki/Pakistani_rupees" class="mw-redirect" title="Pakistani rupees">Rupees</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup> Pakistan also has cyber unit to curb <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography" title="Child pornography">child pornography</a> within the country. The unit has a team of 40 members and one director-level official, who independently investigate the issue. The unit is integrated with the <a href="/wiki/National_Database_and_Registration_Authority" class="mw-redirect" title="National Database and Registration Authority">National Database and Registration Authority</a> (NADRA) and <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Telecommunication_Authority" title="Pakistan Telecommunication Authority">Pakistan Telecommunication Authority</a> (PTA).<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">Philippines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Philippines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_the_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Pornography in the Philippines">Pornography in the Philippines</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The Philippine penal code prohibits the production and distribution of obscene publications. Despite this, enforcement is lax. Some local productions of pornography are known to exist in the country. </p>
      <p>As of January 14, 2017, several pornography sites, mostly mainstream ones such as <a href="/wiki/Pornhub" title="Pornhub">Pornhub</a> and <a href="/wiki/XVideos" title="XVideos">XVideos</a>, have been blocked in the Philippines as part of a government crackdown on child pornography. The Philippine government cites Republic Act 9775 or the Anti-Child Pornography Law as legal justification for the blocks. The list of sites blocked vary depending on the <a href="/wiki/Internet_service_provider" title="Internet service provider">internet service provider</a> enforcing them. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Saudi_Arabia">Saudi Arabia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Saudi Arabia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Items considered pornographic by Saudi Arabian standards are forbidden in the country. Customs authorities enforce strict regulations concerning the importation of pornographic items into Saudi Arabia. Such items may be confiscated on arrival and the owner may be subject to a fine.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup> Accessing pornographic websites can lead to imprisonment, fine, deportation or any other severe punishment by the government.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Syria">Syria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Syria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornography in Syria is illegal and is subject to several legal provisions. The Syrian government began blocking pornography sites in late 2017.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkmenistan">Turkmenistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Turkmenistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Turkmenistan" title="Pornography in Turkmenistan">Pornography in Turkmenistan</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Even though the legal status of pornography in Turkmenistan is unknown, a law, passed on 1 January 2015, banning access to internet pornography<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup> suggests that pornography may be illegal in Turkmenistan. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Vietnam">Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Production, distribution, broadcasting, transport, import and advertisement of pornography, is strictly illegal in Vietnam. In 1996 officials became concerned about pornographic films in the country and launched a campaign, with courts awarding fines and prison sentences. Pornography in Vietnam is classed as a "social evil".<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Europe">Europe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Europe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Europe" title="Pornography in Europe">Pornography in Europe</a>
      </div> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Belarus">Belarus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Belarus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Production, dissemination and assembly of pornography is banned, with laws strictly enforced. Breaking the law is punishable with up to four years in prison.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="France">France</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: France">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In France, pornography is overall permitted, but with distinctions: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>Hardcore pornography must not be sold to minors under the age of 18.</li> 
       <li>Softcore porn is allowed for people 16 and over.</li> 
       <li>Extremely violent or graphic pornography is considered <a href="/wiki/X_rating" title="X rating">X-rated</a>, and so may be shown only in specific theaters, and may not be displayed to <a href="/wiki/Minor_(law)" title="Minor (law)">minors</a>.</li> 
       <li>Some pornography has a special VAT (<a href="/wiki/Value-added_tax" title="Value-added tax">value-added tax</a>): a 33% tax is levied on X-rated movies, and a 50% excise is placed on pornographic online services.</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>The ratings system has caused controversy; e.g., in 2000 the sexually explicit and violent film <i><a href="/wiki/Baise-moi" title="Baise-moi">Baise-moi</a></i> was initially rated only as "restricted" by the French government. This classification was overturned by a <i><a href="/wiki/Conseil_d%27%C3%89tat_(France)" title="Conseil d'État (France)">Conseil d'État</a></i> ruling in a lawsuit brought by associations supporting <a href="/wiki/Christianity" title="Christianity">Christian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Family_values" title="Family values">family values</a>. </p>
      <p>Some movies are forbidden to minors under 18, without the X rating, like <i><a href="/wiki/Baise-moi" title="Baise-moi">Baise-moi</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Ken_Park" title="Ken Park">Ken Park</a></i> or <i><a href="/wiki/Saw_III" title="Saw III">Saw 3</a></i>, so that these movies can be viewed in theaters and not attract VAT. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Germany">Germany</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Germany">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The constitution and law are very strict about <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_pornography" title="Hardcore pornography">hardcore pornography</a>, especially when compared to very liberal laws about <a href="/wiki/Softcore_pornography" title="Softcore pornography">softcore pornography</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prostitution" title="Prostitution">prostitution</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sex_shop" title="Sex shop">sex shops</a>. Supplying hardcore pornography to people who are less than 18 years old is an offence, and shops selling it must keep people under the age of 18 from entering their premises. If only a part of the shop is dedicated to pornography, it must be completely closed off from the rest of the premises. Alternatively, shops may choose not to display their goods or advertise that they sell them, in which case minors may be admitted. Websites hosting pornographic material within Germany must comply with very strict rules about verifying that viewers are over 18.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Soft porn is less restricted, and may even be broadcast on TV at night. The age threshold is usually FSK-16. In contrast many uncut action films or video games easily reach the FSK-18 rating. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungary">Hungary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Hungary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Hungary" title="Pornography in Hungary">Pornography in Hungary</a>
      </div> 
      <p>In Hungary, pornography is unlawful if sold or shown to children under 18 years of age. Displaying genitals openly, as on the cover of a magazine, is not prohibited. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Iceland">Iceland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Iceland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The production or sale of pornography is prohibited in Iceland. Heavy fines were applied in 2001 and ten years earlier a fine was applied to the first manager of the first private TV station (and the only case to present) in Iceland for showing the Danish "mainstream" <a href="/wiki/Zodiac-films" title="Zodiac-films">Zodiac-films</a>, <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=I_Tvillingernes_tegn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="I Tvillingernes tegn (page does not exist)">I Tvillingernes tegn</a></i> and <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=I_Tyrens_tegn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="I Tyrens tegn (page does not exist)">I Tyrens tegn</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup> In early 2013 there was a draft proposal by <a href="/wiki/%C3%96gmundur_J%C3%B3nasson" title="Ögmundur Jónasson">Ögmundur Jónasson</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_the_Interior_(Iceland)" title="Minister of the Interior (Iceland)">Minister of the Interior</a>, to extend the ban to online pornography to protect children from violent sexual imagery.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> The plan has been stalled since the change in government during the <a href="/wiki/Icelandic_parliamentary_election,_2013" class="mw-redirect" title="Icelandic parliamentary election, 2013">parliamentary election on 27 April 2013</a>. Since then, there have been no changes to the relevant legislation, and no changes have been formally proposed.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Italy">Italy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Italy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Italy" title="Pornography in Italy">Pornography in Italy</a>
      </div> 
      <p>In Italy, it is illegal to distribute pictorial or video pornography to persons under the age of 18. However, persons over 18 years of age are permitted to view pornographic material. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">Russia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Russia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>According to Russian law, consumption of pornography is allowed though the production of it is not. The illegal production, distribution, and "public demonstration" of pornography is punishable by a 2- to 6-year prison term. <a href="/wiki/Federal_Service_for_Supervision_of_Communications,_Information_Technology_and_Mass_Media" title="Federal Service for Supervision of Communications, Information Technology and Mass Media">Roskomnadzor</a>, the Russian government's media overseer, has the power to order the blocking of pornographic websites. In 2015 the agency required the blocking of the Russian-language version of <a href="/wiki/Pornhub" title="Pornhub">Pornhub</a> and 10 other pornographic sites on the basis of a court ruling.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>There is nevertheless some uncertainty concerning the legal status of pornography in Russia. The law criminalizes only the 'illegal' production and selling of pornography (which implies that it sometimes can be legal), but two circumstances make enforcement of the law difficult: (1) the lack of a legal definition of pornography, and (2) no law defining when production or selling is permitted.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ukraine">Ukraine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Ukraine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Pornographic production, distribution, broadcasting (both audio and video), transportation, import and advertisement is forbidden by law in Ukraine.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Pornography in the United Kingdom">Pornography in the United Kingdom</a>
      </div> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/England_and_Wales" title="England and Wales">England and Wales</a>, the main legislation on pornographic materials is the <a href="/wiki/Obscene_Publications_Act_1959" title="Obscene Publications Act 1959">Obscene Publications Act 1959</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Obscene_Publications_Act_1964" title="Obscene Publications Act 1964">Obscene Publications Act 1964</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Indecent_Displays_(Control)_Act_1981" title="Indecent Displays (Control) Act 1981">Indecent Displays (Control) Act 1981</a>. Video-oriented depictions of hardcore material (with certain exceptions for works considered primarily 'artistic' rather than pornographic) were banned until 1999, when the removal of trade barriers with other <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> member states allowed for the relatively free movement of such goods for personal use. <a href="/wiki/R18_(British_Board_of_Film_Classification)" title="R18 (British Board of Film Classification)">R18-rated</a> videos are only available in licensed sex shops, but hardcore pornographic magazines are available in shops selling newspapers and magazines. In 2008, the <a href="/wiki/Crown_Prosecution_Service" title="Crown Prosecution Service">Crown Prosecution Service</a> unsuccessfully prosecuted a man under the Obscene Publications Act (the <i><a href="/wiki/R_v_Walker" title="R v Walker">R v Walker</a></i> trial) for a textual story on a pornography website involving <a href="/wiki/Girls_Aloud" title="Girls Aloud">Girls Aloud</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup> Also that year, the <a href="/wiki/Home_Office" title="Home Office">Home Office</a> introduced legislation to criminalize possession of what it has labelled <a href="/wiki/Section_63_of_the_Criminal_Justice_and_Immigration_Act_2008" title="Section 63 of the Criminal Justice and Immigration Act 2008">extreme pornography</a>; these laws are now contained in sections 63 to 68 of the <a href="/wiki/Criminal_Justice_and_Immigration_Act_2008" title="Criminal Justice and Immigration Act 2008">Criminal Justice and Immigration Act 2008</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Oceania">Oceania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Oceania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Censorship_in_Australia" title="Censorship in Australia">Censorship in Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Legal_status_of_Internet_pornography#Australia" title="Legal status of Internet pornography">Legal status of Internet pornography §&nbsp;Australia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography_laws_in_Australia" title="Child pornography laws in Australia">Child pornography laws in Australia</a>
      </div> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, it is legal to possess pornographic material, except child pornography. However, it is illegal to sell, exhibit or rent X-rated pornographic material in all <a href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_Australia" title="States and territories of Australia">states</a> (<a href="/wiki/Victoria_(Australia)" title="Victoria (Australia)">Victoria</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Australia" title="South Australia">South Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tasmania" title="Tasmania">Tasmania</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a>) but it is legal to do so in the two territories (the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Territory" title="Northern Territory">Northern Territory</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Capital_Territory" title="Australian Capital Territory">Australian Capital Territory</a>). As the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Australia" title="Constitution of Australia">Australian constitution</a> prohibits states from regulating interstate commerce, it is permitted to purchase pornography in either territory and then bring it interstate. As a result, the majority of Australian mail-order operations for adult material operate from the ACT.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> Despite the offenses under state laws, stores selling X-rated material are abundant in major cities, advertising openly, as these laws are rarely enforced.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p>
      <p>Ratings for the X18+ category were tightened in 2000 to ban material featuring some fetishes or which appeared to include minors.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> In 2007, the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Territory_National_Emergency_Response" title="Northern Territory National Emergency Response">Northern Territory National Emergency Response</a> introduced by the <a href="/wiki/Howard_Government" title="Howard Government">Howard Government</a> made the possession of RC and X18+ pornography an offence in some Aboriginal communities.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: New Zealand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <table class="box-More_citations_needed_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <td class="mbox-image">
          <div style="width:52px">
           <a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399"></a>
          </div></td>
         <td class="mbox-text">
          <div class="mbox-text-span">
           This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Referencing_for_beginners" title="Help:Referencing for beginners">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">June 2020</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small>
          </div></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, pornography is generally treated in a liberal manner and very little is banned by the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Film_and_Literature_Classification_(New_Zealand)" class="mw-redirect" title="Office of Film and Literature Classification (New Zealand)">Office of Film and Literature Classification</a>. However, the most extreme forms of pornography (such as <a href="/wiki/Child_pornography" title="Child pornography">child pornography</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rape" title="Rape">rape</a>, <a href="/wiki/Incest" title="Incest">incest</a>, <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;"><a href="/wiki/Urophilia" class="mw-redirect" title="Urophilia">urophilia</a></span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> and <a href="/wiki/Bestiality" class="mw-redirect" title="Bestiality">bestiality</a>) are classified as objectionable material by the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Film_and_Literature_Classification_(New_Zealand)" class="mw-redirect" title="Office of Film and Literature Classification (New Zealand)">Office of Film and Literature Classification</a>, effectively banning them.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup> Indecency laws still criminalise some acts under the <a href="/wiki/Crimes_Act_1961" title="Crimes Act 1961">Crimes Act 1961</a>. Pornographic DVDs and magazines that arrive in New Zealand need to be examined by either <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Customs" class="mw-redirect" title="New Zealand Customs">New Zealand Customs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Internal_Affairs" class="mw-redirect" title="Department of Internal Affairs">Department of Internal Affairs</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Police" title="New Zealand Police">New Zealand Police</a> or the Office of Film and Literature Classification before being given an R18 classification. Internet pornography is also regulated but only if websites are based in New Zealand, in which case they will need consent from <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Internal_Affairs" class="mw-redirect" title="Department of Internal Affairs">Department of Internal Affairs</a>. Possession of any material that has objectionable content (which is illegal in New Zealand) is punishable by up to 10 years in jail and a $50,000 fine, or 14 years in jail for distribution of same. Some sex acts are also illegal under the <a href="/wiki/Prostitution_Reform_Act_2003" title="Prostitution Reform Act 2003">Prostitution Reform Act 2003</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Papua_New_Guinea">Papua New Guinea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pornography_laws_by_region&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Papua New Guinea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">Papua New Guinea</a>, the possession, import, export, and sale of pornography are all offenses. Control is strict. According to the government, all websites containing pornography, <a href="/wiki/Nudity" title="Nudity">nudity</a> or depictions of sex are blocked and the government has been blocking such sites since early 2009. Under the law, persons who possess, own, import, export, sell or exhibit pornography to the public are subject to arrest and trial and can face up to 6 months' imprisonment and/or a fine up to 50,000 to 100,000 <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinean_kina" title="Papua New Guinean kina">Papua New Guinean kina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Durham_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Durham-105">[105]</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Self-published_sources" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on a self-published source. (February 2020)">self-published source?</span></a></i>]</sup> In PNG, pornography is subject to legal restraints to publication on grounds of obscenity. Laws relating to pornography in Papua New Guinea are vague. The main legislation used in dealing with cases relating to pornographic nature refer back to the Chapter 262 Criminal Code of Papua New Guinea, Lukautim Pikinini Act 2009, Classification of Publication Censorship Act 1989 and the National ICT Act, 2009. Improper Use of ICT Services.<sup id="cite_ref-Durham_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Durham-105">[105]</a></sup> </p>
